Hi Adam, hi Brian, hi master of the universe, ehm, of PAUSE (do you happen
to have any hints for me on this?), hi everybody!

sorry to bother you, but I couldn't find anything on this in the YAML distr=
o
or on the Net, maybe you can give me a hint what I'm doing wrong? (Certainl=
y
a lot, I know!)

I'd like to provide implementations of the yaml_dump and yaml_load routines
for my Bit::Vector module, and I have done so like this:

sub Bit::Vector::yaml_dump
{
    return "Bit::Vector->new_Hex(" . $_[0]->Size() . ",q{" . $_[0]->to_Hex(=
)
. "})";
}
sub Bit::Vector::yaml_load
{
    if    ($_[0] =3D~
/^Bit::Vector->new_Bin\((\d+),q{(?:0?[bB])?([01]+)}\)$/)        { return
Bit::Vector->new_Bin($1,$2); }
    elsif ($_[0] =3D~
/^Bit::Vector->new_Hex\((\d+),q{(?:0?[xX])?([0-9A-Fa-f]+)}\)$/) { return
Bit::Vector->new_Hex($1,$2); }
    elsif ($_[0] =3D~
/^Bit::Vector->new_Dec\((\d+),q{([+-]?\d+)}\)$/)                { return
Bit::Vector->new_Dec($1,$2); }
    elsif ($_[0] =3D~
/^Bit::Vector->new_Enum\((\d+),q{((?:\d+(?:,\d+)*)?)}\)$/)      { return
Bit::Vector->new_Enum($1,$2); }
    else { return undef; }
}

yaml_dump seems to be partially working, except for a "use of an undefined
value in ..." warning - at least the output
